[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to write [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes to address [0m[1;36m0x00001187a5a0[0m[39m, which is located exactly at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe boundary between two global variables:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The address is [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after the end of `gvcp_register_number` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefined at line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m281[0m[39m, starting at [0m[1;36m0x1187a560[0m[39m, size [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The address is [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes before `gvcp_register_value` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefined at line [0m[1;36m282[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstarting at [0m[1;36m0x1187a5c0[0m[39m, size [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe shadow bytes indicate that the write occurs in a global redzone [0m[1;39m([0m[39mf9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpadding placed between global variables by AddressSanitizer to detect overflows.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following execution path:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer's entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzzshark.c` line [0m[1;36m359[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Packet dissection begins through `epan_dissect_run` and `dissect_record`[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. GVCP protocol dissection starts in `dissect_gvcp` at line [0m[1;36m2766[0m                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Finally reaching the problematic `dissect_register` function at line [0m[1;36m984[0m[39m, column[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer Location**: The `gvcp_register_number` buffer is [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m bytes in size, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe overflow occurs exactly at byte [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset [0m[1;36m0x40[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating an off-by-one or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincorrect index calculation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Write Operation**: A [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte write is being performed, suggesting the code is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting an integer or similar-sized value[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Global Variable**: The affected variables are global, indicating they may be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused across multiple dissection operations and could be arrays or structures for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstoring register information[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Dedup Token**: The token [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"dissect_register--dissect_writereg_cmd--dissect_gvcp"[0m[39m suggests this is a known [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern of vulnerability[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Missing Bounds Checking**: The functions `dissect_register` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m984[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m985[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_extended_bootstrap_register` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1499[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1500[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m write to global arrays [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`gvcp_register_number[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and `gvcp_register_value[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` using `gvcp_register_count` as[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man index without verifying it's within bounds [0m[1;39m([0m[39m< GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT = [0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Counter Reset**: The global variable `gvcp_register_count` is never reset [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m at the start of packet dissection in `[0m[1;35mdissect_gvcp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, causing accumulation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macross multiple packets processed in sequence.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Uncapped Input Validation**: Functions like `dissect_writereg_cmd` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1783[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `dissect_readreg_ack` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2275[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calculate `num_registers` from packet length [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout validating against GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT before iterating.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Attack Vectors:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Single WRITEREG_CMD packet with >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m register-value pairs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength > [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Single READREG_ACK packet with >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m register values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength > [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple sequential packets accumulating >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m total register writes[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- WRITEMEM/READMEM commands calling the vulnerable extended bootstrap register [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix Locations:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Add Bounds Checking in Register Dissection Functions** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCritical[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-gvcp.c` lines [0m[1;36m979[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m985[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mdissect_register[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add a bounds check before writing to the global arrays:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgvcp_register_count >= GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Return failure to indicate array is full[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInsert this check immediately after line [0m[1;36m982[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter reading the value, before [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting to arrays[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-gvcp.c` lines [0m[1;36m1494[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1500[0m[39m in [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdissect_extended_bootstrap_register[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add identical bounds check:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgvcp_register_count >= GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInsert this check immediately after line [0m[1;36m1497[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter reading the value, before [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting to arrays[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Reset Counter at Packet Start** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCritical[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-gvcp.c` around line [0m[1;36m2737[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2740[0m[39m in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdissect_gvcp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Reset the global counter before processing any packet:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgvcp_register_count = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInsert this immediately after line [0m[1;36m2737[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter creating `gvcp_telegram_tree`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore the command/ack branch at line [0m[1;36m2740[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis ensures each packet starts with a clean state and prevents accumulation across[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpackets.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Validate Register Counts Before Loops** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDefense in Depth[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-gvcp.c` line [0m[1;36m1783[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mdissect_writereg_cmd[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add validation after calculating `num_registers`:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint num_registers = length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnum_registers > GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    num_registers = GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Optionally add expert info to indicate truncation[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-gvcp.c` line [0m[1;36m2275[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mdissect_readreg_ack[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add similar validation:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnum_registers = length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnum_registers > GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    num_registers = GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-gvcp.c` line [0m[1;36m1702[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mdissect_readreg_cmd[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough this function doesn't directly cause overflow, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency is important[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint num_registers = length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnum_registers > GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    num_registers = GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification and Rationale[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Approach is Optimal:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: The strategy implements multiple layers of protection:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Counter reset prevents cross-packet accumulation[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Bounds checking prevents any single write from overflowing[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input validation limits loop iterations to prevent excessive calls[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The fixes don't alter the dissection logic or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol handling. They only add safety checks that prevent buffer overflows while [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining all existing functionality.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Performance Impact**: The added checks are simple integer comparisons [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat have negligible performance overhead.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Compatible with Protocol**: Limiting to GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreasonable - if a packet claims more registers than can be stored, processing the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfirst [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m and truncating the rest is safer than crashing. The protocol dissection [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill still succeed for the valid portion.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Harness Modification**: This fix addresses the root cause in the dissector [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode without modifying the fuzzing harness, test infrastructure, or external [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **AddressSanitizer Error**: The bounds checks in `[0m[1;35mdissect_register[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdissect_extended_bootstrap_register[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` directly prevent writing beyond array [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Global Buffer Overflow**: Counter reset ensures `gvcp_register_count` starts at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m for each packet, preventing accumulation beyond [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m across multiple packets.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Scariness Score [0m[1;36m36[0m[39m**: The complete fix eliminates all write-beyond-bounds [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenarios, fully resolving the vulnerability.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Truncation of Large Packets**: Packets with >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m registers will only have the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfirst [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m processed. [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is acceptable for security - the alternative is crashing.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCould optionally add expert info to notify users of truncation.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Early Return from [0m[1;35mdissect_register[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Returning [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m when array is full.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Callers already check return values and handle failures [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgracefully. This maintains consistency with the existing error handling pattern [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., line [0m[1;36m1484[0m[39m returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m for default case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Global State Management**: Still uses global variables.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: While ideally these would be packet-scoped allocations, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanging the architecture is beyond the scope of this security fix. The counter [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreset makes the globals safe for multi-packet processing.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Patterns in Codebase:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe code already has precedent for array bounds limits:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `GVCP_MAX_STREAM_CHANNEL_COUNT` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m512[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is used properly with loop bounds checking [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., line [0m[1;36m2430[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `GVCP_PROTECTED_REGISTER_COUNT` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m properly sizes the `protected_registers[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOur fix applies the same defensive pattern to the vulnerable register arrays.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Considerations:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must not break existing functionality:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Packets with ≤[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m registers: No change in behavior[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Packets with >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m registers: Safely processes first [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, ignores rest[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple sequential packets: Each starts fresh with [0m[33mcounter[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis approach ensures backward compatibility while eliminating the vulnerability.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
